 Michael Debabrata Patra: Patra hoped that demonetisation would have an impact on the economy for a few days, but the threat of global economic and political challenges could persist for a long time
 4
 Ravindra h Dholakia: For the next few months, the increased liquidity with banks due to demonetisation will have a direct impact on the interest rates fixed by it
 vahiin notebandi se arthvyavastha ko jhatka laga he jisase jidipi main growth ke aankalan ko kam karnaa padaa
 However, Dholakia said that it is expected that the impact of demonetisation will last for a few days
 5
 Pami Dua: Dua believed that the country's economy was flexible before demonetisation was implemented

 chetan ghate: notebandi se arthviyavastha main asthirataa badi he

 aapane apane parivaar kaa kharch kyon badhaayaa athwa ghataya?8

 Know 8 tips by which you can crack UPSC interview
 smil:smil ek aisa expressant he jisase aap kisi par apana prabhaav jamaa sakate hai
 Do not take the interview as a task
 ise ek saamaanya daily routine kii tarah len or apane chehre par saamaanya muskaan banaae rakhen
 State your educational qualification: Never leave educational qualification while talking about yourself
 apni padhai or kaam ke bare main zarur bataaen
 Briefly speaking: Generally, in any interview, you are asked to tell your profile and experience
 is samay zyaadaatar ummidavaar bahut hi lanbaa-chaudaa bol jate hai
 Avoid these situations and speak selective things only
 iske liye aap abhi se taiyaari kar len king aapako apane bare main kya bataanaa he or kya nahin
 Explain your wish: Never hide your wish
 ek sawaal jo hameshaa aapse poocha ja saktaa he, wo yah he ki aap is profeshan main kyon aana chaahate hai, aapane puraani job kyon chhodi? in sawaalon ke jawaab ke bare main hameshaa taiyaari karke jaaen
 Talk straight: An attempt to turn the front face with your words can prove to be costly for you, so always speak straight
 apane project, ajukeshan ke bare main khul kar baat karen
 Be clear about the goal: In the interview you can be asked what is the goal regarding your life and profession? In this case, you should not be confused
 sari baaten gambhirtha ke saath kahen
 Know about your post: Keep all the information about the post for which you are going to interview so that there is no problem
 recruiter usee ko recruit karenge, jinhen unke kaam or pad ke bare main pataa he
 Always be natural: Never try to bring any artificial expressions on the face, your body language is also judged in the interview

 swami ne court main kaha ki in dastavejon se congress ke sheersh netaaon par neshnal herald main ghotaalaa sabit ho jaataa he
 In the trial court, Subramanian Swamy presented a copy of the Income Tax Department order sent against the Young Indian Company
 kareeb 105 pannon kii is order copy main kathith taur par neshnal herald par dhokhadhadi kaa aarope lagaaya gaya he
 Swamy also said that this order proves that this conspiracy was hatched to get assets worth 2 thousand crores
 swami ne bataaya ki order main ye bhi kaha gaya he ki congress party ne associats jarnals limited ko 90 karod rupee dene kaa jo daawa kiya he, wo galat he
 No such amount has been given by the party to the AJL
 subramanyam swami ne kaha ki unhone is cese main jo bhi daleelein di thim or aarope lagaae hai, wo is iti order se ekadam sahi sabit hote hai
 Swamy said that the whole deal was a scam
 vahiin jaj ne jirah ke baad cese kii agali sunwaayee ke liye 17 march kaa din mukarrar kiya he
 Also, the court has ordered to keep all documents confidential till the next hearing
 ye he puraa kesaessociats jarnals limited (ageel) neshnal herald akhbaar kii malikana company he
 Congress took its liabilities of Rs 90 crore on 26 February 2011
 iskaa arth ye hua ki party ne ise 90 karod kaa lone de diya
 After this, Young Indian Company was formed with Rs 5 lakh, in which Sonia and Rahul hold 38-38 per cent stake
 baaki kii 24 fisadi hissedari congress netaa motilal vora or auskar furnandis ke paas he
 After this, nine crore shares of Rs 10 each of TAJL were given to 'young Indian' and in return Young Indian was to repay the Congress loan
 9 karod share ke saath yang indian ko is company ke 99 fisadi share hasil ho gaye
 After this, the Congress Party also waived a loan of 90 crores
 yani 'yang indian' ko muft main tiageel kaa swaamitv mil gaya
 bjp's Rajya Sabha MP Subramanian Swamy alleges that all this was done to capture the Rs 16 hundred crore building of Herald House located on Bahadur Shah Zafar Marg in Delhi
 is cese kii sunwaayee dilli ke patiala house court main chal rahi he
 In June 2017, Rahul Gandhi released a memorial publication of National National Herald in Bengaluru
 jiske baad neshnal herald kaa prakaashan phir se shuru ho gaya tha
 The CBI will file a charge sheet against businessman Abhishek Verma and his Romanian wife on August 7
 ek swiss hathiyaar company ko kaali suchi main daalane kii bharat sarkaar kii kaarywahi ko rokane ke liye paise lene ke aarope main donon ko giraftaar kiya gaya he
 CBI prosecutor AK Gaba said before Special Judge Sanjeev Jain here on Wednesday that his investigation in the case is still going on and he will file a charge sheet on August 7
 adaalat ne verma or uski patni anka maaria niksu kii nyaayik hiraasat kii avadhi aath agast tak badha di he
 He was arrested on June 8
 adaalat ne kaha ki jaanch adhikari ne daleel di he ki maamle main padtaal ab bhi chal rahi he
 In this case, the period of judicial custody of both the accused is extended till August 8
 tippaniyan Verma and Anka are accused of taking $ 530,000 from Rainmetal Air Defense AG (RAD)
 bharat sarkaar dwaara company ko kalisuchi main daalane ke liye shuru kii gayi kaarywahi ko rokane ke liye usne kathith taur par apane prabhaav kaa istemaal karne ke liye raashi lee thi
 The CBI has registered cases against him under various sections of the Prevention of Corruption Act
 agar aarope sabit hote hai to unhen chah maah se paanch saal tak kii sajaa ho sakati he
 CBI prosecutor AK Gaba said before Special Judge Sanjeev Jain here on Wednesday that his investigation in the case is still going on and he will file a charge sheet on August 7
 adaalat ne verma or uski patni anka maaria niksu kii nyaayik hiraasat kii avadhi aath agast tak badha di he
 He was arrested on June 8
 adaalat ne kaha ki jaanch adhikari ne daleel di he ki maamle main padtaal ab bhi chal rahi he
 In this case, the period of judicial custody of both the accused is extended till August 8
 tippaniyan Verma and Anka are accused of taking $ 530,000 from Rainmetal Air Defense AG (RAD)
 bharat sarkaar dwaara company ko kalisuchi main daalane ke liye shuru kii gayi kaarywahi ko rokane ke liye usne kathith taur par apane prabhaav kaa istemaal karne ke liye raashi lee thi
